    changelog releases

    Changelog¶

    All notable changes to the Dynamic Alerting Integrations project will be documented in this file.

    [Unreleased]¶

    Changed¶

    • commitlint scope-enum 重整為 deliverable-artifact + cross-cutting 的 18-scope 形狀（v2.8.0, contributor convention） — 32-scope 雜燴砍半，確立 invariant「scope = PR 動到的產品介面 / 長期跨切關注點」。Drop：initiative / phase / 版號 scopes（phase-a/b/c、v2.7.0、v2.8.0）改用 PR labels；compound scopes（dx+e2e、lint+tooling）違反 conventional 的 one-scope 原則；歷史 0–1 次使用的占位 scopes（planning、golden、session-init、config、tooling、adr、scanner、blast-radius、resilience）。Add：tenant-api / portal（先前用 phase-b / jsx 偽裝）、release（取代 chore(v2.X.0) 版號式寫法，對齊 conventional）。Keep：exporter / tools / helm / k8s / rule-packs / docs / ci / e2e / jsx / a11y / dx / ops / lint / audit / playbook。docs/internal/commit-convention.md § Scope 同步重寫（drift check pass）；scripts/tools/dx/pr_preflight.py 動態讀 SOT 不受影響，僅清理 dx+e2e 註解；tests/dx/test_preflight_msg_validator.py 改 anchor 在穩定 scope 而非已 drop 的 config/resilience。

    Added¶

    • Portal ESM build + Vitest unit-test foundation（v2.8.0, TD-030a #247 of TD-030 Option C sweep） — first PR of a multi-PR sweep that retires jsx-loader.html and migrates all 77 portal JSX/JS files to ES modules. This foundation PR is pure infrastructure: tools/portal/build.mjs (esbuild, frontmatter strip, manifest-driven), tools/portal/vitest.config.ts (jsdom + RTL + frontmatter plugin), Makefile targets (portal-build / portal-build-watch / test-portal), new Portal Tests CI job. Manifest starts empty; subsequent PRs (TD-030b..f) add entries as they migrate. jsx-loader.html stays functional for not-yet-migrated tools — TD-030z does the final retirement. User explicitly accepted v2.8.0 release delay as the cost of this architectural cleanup; see project memory project_portal_vitest_choice.md.

    Removed¶

    • components/backstage-plugin/ 整個目錄移除（v2.8.0, Phase .e prep） — v2.1.0 在沒有真實客戶需求前 speculative 寫的 Backstage frontend plugin，14 個月內僅 2 commits（v2.1.0 建立 + v2.6.0 README 微調），長期落後於 v2.5.0+ 的 platform 演進：直連 Prometheus 繞過 v2.5.0/v2.7.0 上線的 tenant-api（沒 RBAC / saved views / SSE / hierarchy resolution），README 列出但程式碼未實作的 feature（alert quality scores、custom/disabled distribution、useMockData config），缺 package.json 不可建置，零測試零 CI 覆蓋（.pre-commit-config.yaml / .github/ / helm/ / tests/ 全無引用）。違反 dev-rule #4 Doc-as-Code（README 與 code 嚴重 drift）。一併清掉 README.md / README.en.md 的 components 列表項 + docs/architecture-and-design.md 專題文件 cross-link；保留 CHANGELOG.md v2.1.0 / v2.6.0 歷史條目 + docs/internal/testing-playbook.md 與 archived lessons-learned.md 的 v2.1.0 LL 紀錄（Entity annotation / proxy CORS pattern 是通用 Backstage 整合知識，與本 plugin 是否存在無關）。未來重做的設計約束：若有真實 Backstage 需求出現，新版應 (1) 走 tenant-api（非直連 Prometheus）取得 RBAC + 完整資料模型，(2) 評估改成 da-tools backstage-export 產 catalog-info.yaml 的 generator 形式（不需追 Backstage SDK 升級、不養 React 程式碼）作為比 plugin 更輕量的選項。

    Security¶

    • Grafana 12.4.1 → 12.4.2（v2.8.0, #98 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump k8s/03-monitoring/deployment-grafana.yaml。audit prerequisite confirmed：configmap-grafana.yaml 唯一 data source 是 Prometheus，無 PostgreSQL，故 12.4.1 帶的 pgx/v5 CVE-2026-33816（CRITICAL memory-safety, fixed in 5.9.0）在我們部署是 dead-code。bump 主要修 12.4.1 → 12.4.2 自身的 Go binary CVE（含 grpc CVE-2026-33186 transitive）。Trivy 0.70.0 audit：Go binary 部分 8/2 → 7/1（pgx 那條 CRITICAL 即使可達也已被 12.4.2 fix）。殘留 11 HIGH + 2 CRITICAL Alpine OS layer（OpenSSL/libssl3/musl/zlib）upstream Grafana 還沒 rebase Alpine 3.22+，CRITICAL CVE-2026-31789 是 32-bit only（amd64 N/A），HIGH OpenSSL CMS path 在 Grafana 不啟用 — 留 issue 追 upstream rebase。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    • Prometheus + Alertmanager stack bump（v2.8.0, #96 + #97 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump 4 處 image refs 對齊 prom/ monitoring stack：k8s/03-monitoring/deployment-prometheus.yaml v3.10.0 → v3.11.2、k8s/03-monitoring/deployment-alertmanager.yaml v0.31.1 → v0.32.0、tests/e2e-bench/docker-compose.yml 的 prometheus v2.55.0 → v3.11.2（Prometheus 2.x 已 EOL 2024-12-03）+ alertmanager v0.27.0 → v0.32.0。Trivy 0.70.0 audit 2026-04-26：清掉 grpc CVE-2026-33186（CRITICAL memory-safety）+ Go stdlib 1.25.7 / 1.26.0 → 1.26.2 升級涵蓋的全部 CVE-2026-32280/281/283 等 + e2e-bench 那組 v2.55.0 帶的 11 個 stdlib CVE（Go 1.23.2 → 1.26.2）+ x/crypto CVE-2024-45337（CRITICAL SSH misuse, fixed in v0.31.0）。Prometheus k8s 9 HIGH + 1 CRITICAL → 3 HIGH + 0 CRITICAL（殘留 jsonparser/moby authz/otel BSD-only，皆不可達）；Alertmanager k8s 6 HIGH + 1 CRITICAL → 1 HIGH + 0 CRITICAL（殘留 otel-go kenv path 是 BSD-only）。e2e-bench compose 改 v3.x 後 18 HIGH + 3 CRITICAL → 3 HIGH + 0 CRITICAL（同 k8s 殘留）。注意*：Prometheus 2.x → 3.x 是 major bump，但本 PR 用到的 flags（--config.file、--web.enable-lifecycle、--storage.tsdb.retention.time）都仍向下相容；現有 prometheus.yml / alert-rules.yml 格式無 breaking change。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    • oauth2-proxy v7.7.1/v7.15.1 → v7.15.2（v2.8.0, #92 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump 5 個 image references 對齊到單一版本：k8s/04-tenant-api/deployment.yaml（從 v7.7.1 跳兩個 minor）、helm/da-portal/values{,-tier1,-tier2}.yaml 與 helm/tenant-api/values.yaml（從 v7.15.1）。clear 三條 auth bypass：CVE-2026-34457（CRITICAL：health-check User-Agent matching 繞 auth_request mode）、CVE-2026-40575（CRITICAL：X-Forwarded-Uri header spoofing）、GHSA-pxq7-h93f-9jrg（HIGH：fragment confusion in skip_auth_routes）。Trivy 0.70.0 audit 2026-04-26：v7.7.1 帶 16 HIGH + 6 CRITICAL（含早期 CVE-2025-54576 fixed in 7.11.0）、v7.15.1 帶 6 HIGH + 2 CRITICAL；target v7.15.2 在 trivy 上 0 / 0 clean（Debian 13.4 + go binary 全乾淨）。修掉 v7.7.1 vs v7.15.1 的 inter-file drift。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    • alpine/git init container 2.43.0 → v2.52.0（v2.8.0, #93 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump tenant-api init container 在 k8s/04-tenant-api/deployment.yaml + helm/tenant-api/templates/deployment.yaml。clear 8 個 git binary CVE 含 4 個 RCE/exfil class：CVE-2024-32002（CRITICAL recursive-clone RCE）、CVE-2024-32004（local clone RCE）、CVE-2024-32021（symlink bypass）、CVE-2024-32465（local RCE）、CVE-2024-52006（credential exfil via newline confusion）、CVE-2025-46334、CVE-2025-48384（RCE）、CVE-2025-48385（arbitrary file write）。Trivy 0.70.0 audit：current 32 HIGH + 4 CRITICAL → target 13 HIGH + 2 CRITICAL（殘留全是 Alpine 3.23.3 OS layer，但 init container 只 clone 受信任內網 GitOps repo，OpenSSL DoS / CMS 殘留 CVE 不可達）。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    • Python base image 3.13.3 → 3.13.13-alpine3.22（v2.8.0, #94 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump components/da-tools/app/Dockerfile（builder + runtime）+ tests/e2e-bench/driver/Dockerfile（順手把 floating python:3.13-alpine 釘到 explicit version 取得 reproducibility）。Trivy 0.70.0 audit 2026-04-26：current python:3.13.3-alpine3.22 帶 15 HIGH + 5 CRITICAL（含 CVE-2025-15467 OpenSSL pre-auth RCE、CVE-2025-6965 sqlite integer truncation、CVE-2025-48174/48175 libavif、CVE-2026-31789 OpenSSL heap overflow on 32-bit）；target image 在 trivy 上 0 / 0 clean（Alpine 3.22.4 patched + Python 3.13.13 stdlib fixes）。da-tools Dockerfile 既有的 RUN apk --no-cache upgrade 仍保留作 defense-in-depth。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    • Go toolchain 1.26.1 → 1.26.2（v2.8.0, #95 of umbrella #100 Q2 2026 CVE audit） — bump 三份 go.mod (components/tenant-api、components/threshold-exporter/app、tests/e2e-bench/receiver) + 對應 3 份 Dockerfile 從 floating golang:1.26-alpine 釘到 golang:1.26.2-alpine3.22。一次清掉 10 個 stdlib CVE：CVE-2026-33810（Go 1.26 only x509 wildcard bypass）、CVE-2026-27140（cmd/go SWIG cgo trust-layer bypass，build-time RCE）、CVE-2026-32289（html/template XSS）、CVE-2026-32282（os.Root.Chmod symlink traversal）、CVE-2026-32283（TLS 1.3 key-update DoS）、CVE-2026-32280/32281（crypto/x509 DoS）、CVE-2026-32288（archive/tar unbounded allocation）、CVE-2026-27143/27144（cmd/compile memory corruption + type confusion）。Trivy 0.70.0 audit 2026-04-26 confirm。詳見 #100 audit 摘要。

    Fixed¶

    • /api/v1/me JSON wire shape: nil-vs-empty-array drift（v2.8.0, TD-028 #242） — schemathesis contract test (TD-022) caught two Response violates schema failures on GET /api/v1/me: when caller had no group memberships, groups and accessible_tenants serialised as null even though the OpenAPI spec declared both as array. Root cause: rbac.RequestGroups(r) returns nil when the X-Forwarded-Groups header is absent, and accessibleTenants was only populated by appending to a nil slice. Fix: in internal/handler/me.go, normalise groups to []string{} when nil and explicitly initialise resp.AccessibleTenants = []string{} so the JSON encoder emits [] not null. Added wire-level regression test TestMe_EmptyGroupsRendersAsArray that asserts on the encoded body string ("groups":[]), not the Go struct field, because the failure mode is encoding-side. CI integration enabled in same PR: make contract-test now runs in Go Tests (1.26) after the swag drift check (CONTRACT_MAX_EXAMPLES=5, ~10–20s). Two known warnings remain (input-side pattern missing on path params + example values for IDs) — non-blocking and tracked as follow-up.

    • check_head_blob_hygiene.py regression tests + hang-localization milestones + S#74 lesson codify（v2.8.0, follow-up to PR #164） — PR #164 fixed the _batch_cat_blobs Popen deadlock in flight while shipping PR-2c, but did not include tests or codify the agent-discipline lesson that surfaced. This PR closes those gaps and adds the "仍待：progress output" item that Trap #57 had been carrying since v2.8.0 Phase .a. 20 new tests in tests/lint/test_check_head_blob_hygiene.py: 3 deadlock-regression (small batch sanity / large batch 1000×2KB regression-catcher / empty input — using a real on-disk git repo fixture, not mocks, since the deadlock is in the real Popen pipe interaction), 2 output-parsing, 4 scan_blob rule (NUL / EOF strict-only / TRUNC mkdocs-yml), 3 hang-localization milestone tests (default-mode "Reading N..." + "batch read complete" + per-100 scan progress; --verbose per-file scan progress), 8 _is_skippable parametrized. Tests run in ~6.4s locally. Three layers of regression defense: (1) @pytest.mark.timeout(N) per-test pytest-level fast-fail (added pytest-timeout to CI deps), (2) explicit elapsed-time soft-budget assertion, (3) inner communicate(timeout=60) in the function under test. Empirical dogfood verified the regression test catches the regression by intentionally reverting _batch_cat_blobs back to the write-then-read-loop pattern, observing the headline test timeout at 120s (pytest-timeout firing), then restoring — without this loop the test would have been an article-of-faith. Notable empirical finding: 300×1KB total output does NOT reliably trigger the deadlock on Windows (pipe buffer happens to absorb it); reliable trigger threshold is ~1000+ paths, captured in the headline test parameters. Hang-localization milestones now baked into the hook itself: prints Reading N HEAD blob(s)... → ✓ batch read complete: N loaded in Xs → ...scanned I/N every 100 in default mode → final summary. Three observation points let an operator pin down "is it stuck before the batch read, in the batch read, or in the per-blob scan" without re-running with --verbose — closes the diagnostic-gap that Trap #57 had been waiting on since 2026-04-23. Trap #57 in windows-mcp-playbook.md updated from "🟡 Mitigated" to "🟢 Resolved": (a) second root-cause class (Popen pipe deadlock, orthogonal to FUSE stale-temp class) documented with identification rules (NTFS → 100% Popen; FUSE + phantom → stale temp; FUSE + clean phantom → likely Popen), (b) hang-localization milestones documented as the diagnostic path. testing-playbook.md v2.8.0 Lessons §4 (NEW) codifies S#74: subprocess hang requires an SLA prior + escalation policy, not patience. Three-step escalation: (a) ps -ef | grep <suspect> to locate the live subprocess, (b) isolate and reproduce the stuck path standalone, (c) instrument the suspect path. Plus a verify-reference extension to S#73: hook scripts authored by others are not exempt — read the critical paths (Popen / pipe / I/O) before assuming "it works".

    • check_head_blob_hygiene.py Popen deadlock above ~150 paths（v2.8.0, lint, discovered while shipping PR-2c） — the _batch_cat_blobs helper used a single-threaded write-then-read-loop pattern over git cat-file --batch --buffer's stdin/stdout pipes. With --buffer git accumulates ALL stdout in memory until stdin EOF then flushes at once; once total output exceeded the OS pipe buffer (~64KB on Windows) git blocked on stdout write while the script was still reading from a different path's body bytes — classic single-thread Popen pipe deadlock. Symptom: pre-commit hook HEAD blob hygiene (NUL bytes / truncated structured files) hung indefinitely on every commit (the repo passed 1040 tracked files with ~2.18MB of cat-file output, well over the deadlock threshold). Fix: replace manual write-then-read with proc.communicate(input=request, timeout=60), which uses internal threads to drain stdout/stderr while writing stdin — sidestepping the deadlock without changing semantics (we already buffered all output in memory for the parse loop anyway). Output parsing rewritten as in-memory byte-buffer walk over the bytes returned by communicate(). After fix: --ci run completes in 0.57s for 1040 blobs (was indefinite hang). 60s timeout + try/except on OSError and TimeoutExpired ensures the script can never hang the commit again — empty-result fallback to per-path _cat_blob loop preserved. Net regression unblock: every commit was previously hanging on this hook for sufficiently large repos; this restores the hook to its intended fast-path. Discovered while shipping PR-2c — included here rather than as a separate PR because the bug was actively blocking the commit.

    • TestSlowWriteTornStateStress race-flake hardening — quiescence detection rewrite（v2.8.0, Phase B testing follow-up, closes #157） — B-7 slow-write torn-state stress 從 v2.8.0 cycle 起 flaked CI 兩次（PR #151 + PR #155 各 1 次），symptom 都是 sliding debounce violated: fire count = 1 after write 19/2 (expected 0 throughout the burst)。這 PR 不修 production code — debounce 沒 bug；修的是 test 違反了 PR #149 codify 的 testing-playbook lesson §2 anti-pattern：for { trigger; t.Sleep(jitter) } + assert fireCount == 0 是 wall-clock 斷言，loaded CI runner overshooting sleep 就會誤判 burst split。

    • 修法：完整套用 lesson §2 canonical quiescence pattern：
      • 移除 mid-burst fireSnapshots 抽樣 + 「expected 0 throughout the burst」斷言（這條是 timing claim，不是 contract claim）
      • 移除 post-settle time.Sleep(2*window) + assert fireCount == 1（同樣 timing claim）
      • 加入新 helper waitForQuiescence(t, deadline, stableWindow, counterFn) — 輪詢計數器直到 stableWindow 連續 ms 沒變動，否則 timeout
      • Post-quiescence assert 三條 contract-stable invariants：(1) debounceBatch._sum == numFiles（每個 trigger 都 coalesce 到某個 fire — 抓 lost-trigger）；(2) merged_hash 全 tenant 從 baseline 推進（抓 lost-write）；(3) _count ≤ 2 CI-jitter envelope（外面就是真 broken debounce）
      • fireCount 變 informational logging — 不再硬斷言
    • 重新命名：TestSlowWriteTornStateStress_FinalConvergenceNoTornFires → TestSlowWriteTornStateStress_FinalConvergence — 誠實對應改寫後的合約（drop 「NoTornFires」承諾，因 fireCount 不再硬斷）。File 開頭加段 issue #157 history block 給 future reader 知道改寫 rationale
    • 驗證：本機 dev-container -race -count=10 全綠（vs. 改寫前 CI 上 ~每 10-15 PR 觸發 1 次）；regression 注入「skip every-other trigger」bug → test FAIL at _sum=25 != 50，確認 invariants 仍能抓到 lost-trigger class

    • 第三條 worked example 加進 testing-playbook.md §v2.8.0 Lessons Learned — Race-flake battles lesson §2 — 跟 PR #79 / #90 兩個 worked example 並列，強化 visibility

    • tenant-api body-content range validation 在邊界 fail-fast（v2.8.0, Phase B Track C C4 deferred, closes #134） — Track C 期間明示 deferred 至獨立 PR 處理的 C4 項目落地。v2.8.0 之前的 POST /api/v1/tenants/batch / PUT /api/v1/groups/{id} / PUT /api/v1/views/{id} body 只驗 size (≤1MB) + JSON 格式，不驗值範圍 — customer 送 {"_timeout_ms":"99999999999"} 之類的 nonsense value，API 直接通過寫進 git，幾分鐘後 downstream（threshold-exporter resolve / GitOps writer YAML parse）才 reject。客戶看到的錯誤訊息位置離犯錯點極遠，debug 成本高，且 bad write 已經進 git 需要 revert PR。

    • 修法：新增 components/tenant-api/internal/handler/body_validator.go，hybrid 設計：
      • Fixed-shape 欄位（Label / Description / Members）用 go-playground/validator/v10 struct tags：validate:"required,min=1,max=256" / validate:"max=4096" / validate:"max=1000,dive,min=1,max=256"
      • Variable-shape Patch map[string]string 用 imperative per-key validator registry：reservedKeyValidators 對 _silent_mode / _timeout_ms / _quench_min / _routing_profile / _profile 分別 enum-check 或 numeric-bound-check
      • Soft whitelist 政策：未在 registry 的 _* 開頭 reserved key 通過（generic length cap 仍適用），避免 tenant-api 跟 threshold-exporter release cadence 過度耦合 — 新 reserved key 加進 threshold-exporter 不需先發 tenant-api 版本
      • 兩條路徑都產出同一個 Violation{Field, Reason} shape，feed 進 writeValidationErrors 統一 JSON response
    • Response shape（per #134 spec）：{error: "validation failed", code: "INVALID_BODY", violations: [{field, reason}]} — violations 列全部錯誤（不是 first-only），跟 Track C PR-2 forbidden-member 列表 UX 一致，客戶 1 個 round-trip 就能 fix 完
    • Reserved-key 規則 SOT cross-checked threshold-exporter config_resolve.go (_silent_mode 4 個 valid value 對齊 {warning, critical, all, disable}，case-insensitive)；_timeout_ms 上限 1h、_quench_min 上限 1d 對齊 ADR 慣例
    • Generic length cap：所有 patch key ≤ 256 chars，所有 patch value ≤ 1024 chars，Filters value ≤ 1024 chars — 擋掉 multi-MB blob 貼進 value 的 resource-exhaustion vector
    • 新 body_validator_test.go（19 cases，全綠 + -race -count=1）：
      • validateSilentMode 9 cases（4 valid + case-insensitive + empty + off-rejected + nonsense）
      • validateNonNegativeIntCap 6 fail cases（含 #134 issue 範例 99999999999）+ pass cases
      • validateNonEmptyString256 4 cases 含 256-char boundary
      • validatePatchMap 7 cases：valid passthrough / single violation / multiple violations all reported / unknown reserved key passthrough / oversized key / oversized value / boundary numeric (3600000 pass, 3600001 fail)
      • validateStructTags 4 cases 對 BatchRequest / PutGroupRequest
      • validateFilterMap 2 cases
      • writeValidationErrors JSON shape contract
      • BatchTenants handler integration 2 cases — 確認 validation 跑在 RBAC / per-op work 之前，full violation list 都列出
    • Existing tests 全 pass：13 個 TestPutGroup_* / TestPutView_* 不變（struct-tag 鬆嚴度跟原本 if req.Label == "" 一致，沒 break 既有 happy/sad path）

    • Mixed-mode benchmarks 加入 nightly bench-record cron（v2.8.0, Phase B Track B follow-up, issue #128 prerequisite） — Track B 期間 Phase B PR 落地 4 個 mixed-mode benchmarks（BenchmarkScanDirHierarchical_MixedMode_500flat_500hier / BenchmarkFullDirLoad_MixedMode_500flat_500hier / BenchmarkDiffAndReload_MixedMode_500flat_500hier_NoChange / BenchmarkFullDirLoad_MixedMode_100flat_900hier），但 Phase 1 baseline 的 make benchmark-report 用 -bench='_1000(_|$)' 過濾，4 個 mixed-mode 名稱結尾為 _500hier / _900hier / _NoChange 全 miss。結果 nightly bench-record.yaml workflow 從未真正量過 mixed mode — issue #128 等的「authoritative numbers ... 28+ data points」start clock 從未起跑。

    • 修法：Makefile benchmark-report 的 -bench regex 從 _1000(_|$) 擴成 _1000(_|$)|MixedMode，把 4 個 mixed-mode 帶進來。原 13 benches (8 flat + 5 hierarchical) → 17 benches (+ 4 mixed-mode)，nightly artifact 從這次 cron 起含 mixed-mode 數據
    • 影響範圍：make benchmark-report 改變 → 自動 propagate 到 (a) nightly bench-record.yaml workflow（自動，由 cron 觸發）；(b) pre-tag make pre-tag chain（手動，下次 tag 時 baseline 會多 4 條）；(c) release-attach-bench-baseline.yaml 自動 attach 到 GitHub Release 的 bench-baseline-<tag>.txt。下游 analyze_bench_history.py 不假設特定 bench 數量（grep ^Benchmark...-N\s+\d+\s 樣式），相容
    • 時間預算：nightly cron 一輪預估從 ~10-15 min ramp 到 ~12-18 min（4 個 mixed-mode 的 fixture-setup + 各 count=6 × benchtime=3s ≈ 18-72s extra），仍在 timeout 30 min 之內
    • wall-clock 計時：本 PR landed 之後第一次 nightly 為「Day 1」；累積至 28+ 點數據（~28 天 wall-clock，target ~2026-05-29）後可由 #128 acceptance 跑 analyze_bench_history.py 統計判讀，決定 mixed mode 是否需 perf optimization PR
    • 本 PR 不關閉 #128：本 PR 是 #128 的 prerequisite —「啟動 wall-clock 累積」；真正關閉 #128 需要等 28 天後拿到統計判讀。但 issue body 可在 PR merge 後 update 加上「nightly 已從 PR #XXX 啟動，data accumulating from {date}」

    • 同步更新 docs/internal/github-release-playbook.md 對應「13 benches × count=6」描述為「17 benches × count=6（包含 4 mixed-mode 自 issue #128 加入後）」+ runner 時間預估同步

    • threshold-exporter mixed-mode duplicate tenant ID 從 WARN 升 hard error（v2.8.0, Phase B Track B follow-up, issue #127） — 同一 tenant ID 同時出現在 flat 路徑（<root>/<id>.yaml）+ nested 路徑（<root>/<dir>/<id>.yaml）時，v2.8.0 之前的行為是 flat-mode loadDir 已 silently last-wins-merge → populateHierarchyState 抓到 duplicate 但只 emit WARN log（config.go L194）→ Load() 回傳 nil。客戶部署一個帶 duplicate 的 conf.d 看似成功但實際 tenant 內容是 map 迭代順序決定的「last-wins」，極易在 production 漏察。

    • 修法：新增 typed error *DuplicateTenantError（config_hierarchy.go，含 TenantID / PathA / PathB 欄位），scanDirHierarchical 改回 typed error 取代 generic fmt.Errorf。Load() 與 fullDirLoad() 用 errors.As 區分：duplicate-tenant misconfig propagate 為 hard error，generic scan errors（permissions / malformed file）仍走原本 log-and-continue 政策（hierarchical mode 是 opt-in，半個 malformed 分支不該擊倒整個 flat-only deploy）
    • 狀態 invariant：cold-start Load() 拒絕時 m.config / m.loaded 維持 pre-Load 值（nil / false），無 partial state 洩漏。Hot-reload fullDirLoad() 拒絕時保留 prior 已知正常狀態 — 跑著的 service 不會被半途切換到 broken state
    • scanDirHierarchical 順序調整：Load() / fullDirLoad() 都把 populateHierarchyState() 呼叫移到 flat-mode commit 之前，確保拒絕時不需 unwind 已 swap 的 m.config
    • 新 config_mixed_mode_test.go test：TestMixedMode_DuplicateAcrossModes_RejectedAtLoad 取代原本 _DetectedButNotPropagated 鎖死 v2.8.0 之前 gap 的 test；驗證新合約四要點（hard error / errors.As 解出 typed error / 兩條路徑都 populated 且 distinct / 拒絕時無 state 洩漏）。新增 TestMixedMode_DuplicateAcrossModes_RejectedAtFullDirLoad 鎖 hot-reload 路徑，驗證 reload 拒絕後 m.config / m.lastHash 仍指向 prior known-good 狀態

Lessons learned during the sweep, captured in PR descriptions for future reference: (1) purpose: blocks in YAML front-matter must NOT contain --- separator lines (the ^---[\s\S]*?---\s*\n? strip regex matches them as the closing FM marker, leaving partial FM as code → Babel parse error); (2) JSX inline style={{ ... }} patterns trigger the manual-stage jsx-babel-check-strict-linecount hook (browser-mode Babel.transformScriptTags silently strips inner object literals); fix is module-scope const XXX_STYLE = { ... } + style={XXX_STYLE} indirection; (3) sed-damage-guard heuristic blocks legitimate large refactors that shrink files > 50% in-place — workaround is incremental decomposition keeping orchestrator above 50% of original size, OR additive-only PRs that defer shim conversion. Cross-refs: #203, #204, #205, #206.

    • toBeVisibleWithDiagnostics matcher + testing-playbook §LL §11 Tier 1 reframe + §LL §12 NEW closed-vs-open enumeration discipline（v2.8.0, lint architecture self-correction, S#98） — replaces S#97 PR #187 (closed unmerged) which attempted Tier 1 of §LL §11 as commit-time enumeration lint. User review caught the architectural mistake before merge: input-establishment enumeration is open-set whack-a-mole (Playwright keeps adding interaction methods, custom helpers wrap them, mental-model mismatch failure modes are countless beyond cold-start). The right shape for open-set bug classes is runtime diagnostic feedback at assertion-failure time, not commit-time pattern-list maintenance. tests/e2e/fixtures/diagnostic-matchers.ts (~140 LoC): drop-in toBeVisibleWithDiagnostics() matcher — success path identical to .toBeVisible() (zero overhead); failure path collects every data-testid currently visible on the page via page.evaluate(...) over getBoundingClientRect and dumps them in the assertion error message. ZERO enumeration, no pattern list to maintain, works for every Playwright version + custom helper + state-machine pattern. Catches every mental-model mismatch class — cold-start (PR #185), async race, validation reject, stale mock, re-mount, selector miss. Adoption pattern: opt-in side-effect import import './fixtures/diagnostic-matchers' at spec top + .toBeVisibleWithDiagnostics() at call site (gradual adoption, non-state assertions stay regular .toBeVisible()). tests/e2e/diagnostic-matchers-self-test.spec.ts (3 scenarios): pass-through (visible locator, no error) + failure-with-testids (synthetic data-URL page with 3 visible + 1 hidden testid → matcher's failure message contains all 3 visible names AND NOT the hidden one) + failure-with-empty-page (zero testids → "JSX component mount" hint, different bug class). Demonstration: simulate-preview.spec.ts 3 state- assertions (auto-simulates / 4xx error / network failure — exactly the 3 PR #185 first-CI-fail cases) swapped to .toBeVisibleWithDiagnostics(). testing-playbook §LL §11 Tier 1 reframe (changed kind, ⏸️→🟢): Tier 1 v2 = matcher not enumeration lint; Tier 2/3 deferred indefinitely (redundant with Tier 1 v2). testing-playbook §LL §12 NEW "Closed-vs-open enumeration discipline check": rule of thumb — before writing a lint, ask if the target set is closed; closed (lint OK; e.g. RTL getBy* family per S#96 PR #186, JSX-loader allowlist per S#93) vs open (Playwright interaction methods, state-marker testid suffixes, CSS-in-JS class names, custom helpers — lint = whack-a-mole). 3-question decision tree + 4 alternative architectures for open-set classes (runtime diagnostic / convention forcing / snapshot baselines / read-time review checklist) + 3 anti-patterns. Canonical contrast: S#96 PR #186 (closed-set ✓ correct shape) vs S#97 PR #187 (open-set ✗ wrong shape, closed unmerged). Net delta vs S#97*: -340 LoC enumeration lint + 49 tests + ongoing pattern-list maintenance burden → +140 LoC matcher + 80 LoC self-test + zero ongoing maintenance. Cross-refs: PR #185 fix commit 3beb127 (motivating cold-start incident), PR #187 closed unmerged (the wrong-shape lint), §LL §11 (Tier 1 v2 reframe), §LL §12 (the discipline rule that fell out of the self-correction).

    • check_jsx_loader_compat.py lint + testing-playbook LL §9 codify（v2.8.0, lint hardening, S#93） — codifies the S#92 PR #182 amend lesson into a mechanical commit-time gate. Root cause that this lint catches: jsx-loader's Babel-standalone runs in script mode, where named exports compile to exports.x = ... which fails at runtime (ReferenceError: exports is not defined); React tree never mounts. pre-commit run jsx-babel-check only PARSES JSX (export function is a valid AST node), so the syntactic gate doesn't catch this — only CI E2E does. Three rule classes, all FATAL: (1) named-export — ^export (function|const|let|var|class) (NOT export default); (2) non-allowlist-import — import ... from '<X>' where X ∉ {react, lucide-react} (the only two sources jsx-loader's transformImports() regex handles per docs/assets/jsx-loader.html lines ~624-638); (3) require-call — \brequire\s*\( calls. Per-line escape via <!-- jsx-loader-compat: ignore --> (3-line lookback). Live audit at codify time: 0 violations across 49 JSX files (S#92 fix already merged). Pre-merge intentional-break dogfood: re-introduced the historical PR #182 root cause (function computeTrace → export function computeTrace) → lint immediately caught at routing-trace.jsx:80:1 [named-export] → restored. testing-playbook §v2.8.0 LL §9 codifies the full constraint surface (5 ✅ allowed + 5 ❌ banned patterns) + cross-refs to jsx-loader.html transformImports source-of-truth + jsx-multi-file-pattern.md for cross-tool reuse correct path. 47 unit tests covering all 3 rules + allowlist + 3-line ignore lookback + multi-rule on same source + comment skip + main() integration. 7th dogfood of make lint-extract scaffold (text kind). Pre-commit hook jsx-loader-compat-check auto-stage FATAL; tool count 136 → 137. Cross-refs: PR #182 amend 6e16a65 (real-world failure); LL §9 (constraint codify).

    • C-3 PR-3 — routing-trace wizard — C-3 軌道完結（v2.8.0, Phase .c, S#92） — retires the LAST "Planned v2.8.x" badge on Master Onboarding Wizard Journey step 4 by shipping a real routing-trace.jsx 4-step Alertmanager routing simulator. Wizard Journey 5/5 real wizards complete: cicd-setup → deployment → alert-builder → routing-trace → tenant-manager. Steps: (1) Sample alert — alertname (PascalCase validated) + severity (warning/critical/info) + extra labels；(2) Default route — top-level receiver + group_by labels；(3) Child routes — list of {match labels, receiver} blocks, + Add Child Route to grow, ✕ to remove；(4) Trace result — matched route hierarchy + final receiver + ordered reasoning trace + copy-to-clipboard. Routing algorithm: walks child routes top-to-bottom; first whose match labels are ALL satisfied (AND semantics) wins; otherwise falls through to default receiver. Pure function computeTrace({ alert, defaultRoute, childRoutes }) exported for reuse + testability. Honest scope (matches alert-builder PR-2 pattern)：form-driven only, NO arbitrary YAML parsing (avoids vendor dep), NO regex matchers (match_re / matchers constraint syntax), NO nested route trees (single-level child routes), NO continue: true semantics, NO timing simulation (group_wait / group_interval / repeat_interval), NO inhibit rules (orthogonal — alert-simulator already has inhibit preview, surfaced in step 3 integration tips). The wizard teaches the routing CONCEPT (label match → tree walk → receiver) without trying to be a complete Alertmanager simulator (use amtool for that). Master Onboarding wiring change: step 4 deferred: true → removed; href routing-profiles.md → routing-trace.html; "Planned" badge gone.     • C-3 PR-2 — alert-builder wizard（v2.8.0, Phase .c, S#91） — retires the "Planned v2.8.x" badge on Master Onboarding Wizard Journey step 3 by shipping a real alert-builder.jsx 4-step wizard. Steps: (1) Identity — alertName (PascalCase validated) + groupName + summary annotation；(2) Expression — PromQL textarea + comparison op (6 options) + threshold (numeric validated) + for-duration (preset chips + free input)；(3) Severity — warning / critical / info choice + extra labels (key=value pairs, lowercase-key convention WARN) + optional description annotation；(4) Review — generated PrometheusRule YAML in pre block + copy-to-clipboard + integration tips. Output is a complete groups: [{name, rules: [{alert, expr, for, labels, annotations}]}] snippet ready for rule-packs/<x>.yaml paste or da-tools alert-create feed.     • check_subprocess_timeout.py — S#74 Code-driven Layer A lint（v2.8.0, lint, follow-up to PR #165） — codifies S#74's "subprocess hang must have an SLA" lesson into AST-based lint. Flags two heuristic classes: (a) subprocess.{run, call, check_call, check_output}(...) without timeout= kwarg or with timeout=None / timeout=0 / timeout=0.0 (functionally equivalent to no timeout), (b) <expr>.communicate(...) without meaningful timeout= (the canonical Popen.communicate hang-prone API; PR #164's deadlock was exactly this pattern). Per-line ignore via # subprocess-timeout: ignore marker (3-line lookback for multi-line rationale comment blocks). Granular --strict-subprocess-timeout flag (mirrors PR #162's --strict-static / --strict-linecount split): codebase audit shows 90 existing violations across 33 files as of v2.8.0 (raw grep matches 218 sites; the delta is comments / strings / docstrings filtered out by AST walk + 3 silenced via self-dogfood); cleaning all of them in one PR is impractical, so the lint ships warn-only by default under --ci and only becomes fatal under --ci --strict-subprocess-timeout. Future PR (tracked in Issue #167) will activate the strict flag once the cleanup track lands. 55 unit tests covering: detection rules (4 subprocess fns × parametrized + 4 communicate variants + Popen-constructor-not-flagged + bare-imported-not-flagged), timeout value semantics (None / 0 / 0.0 flagged; positive int / float / variable / expression accepted), ignore-comment behavior (call-line / 3-line lookback / outside-lookback rejection), robustness (syntax-error survival + string-literal-not-flagged + comment-not-flagged), file discovery (_iter_python_files recursion / .py filter / sort / nonexistent-root), path resolution (_resolve_scan_paths absolute / relative / fallback), main() end-to-end (clean / warn-only / strict-fatal / no-ci), 4-state severity matrix truth table (--ci × --strict-subprocess-timeout × n_violations 0/N → exit code), and report shape. All run in 0.37s. Pre-commit hook subprocess-timeout-audit (auto-stage, warn-only, files ^(scripts|components/da-tools|tests)/.*\.py$) — surfaces violation count on every commit without blocking, matching the cleanup-track convention from PR #162. Self-dogfood: PR #165's tests/lint/test_check_head_blob_hygiene.py had 3 fixture-side subprocess.run(["git", ...]) calls flagged; silenced via # subprocess-timeout: ignore markers, demonstrating the UX in production code (and dropping the audit count from 93 → 90). The 3-line lookback feature was added after I personally hit the 1-line limit on a multi-line rationale comment — turning the footgun discovery into a UX improvement before merge. Pre-merge self-review pass 2 (user-prompted) found 3 real gaps: (i) timeout=None/0 slipping past the structural check (fixed: _has_meaningful_timeout now value-aware), (ii) _iter_python_files / _resolve_scan_paths / main() had no direct tests — only via parametrized helpers — added 11 tests + 1 robustness fix in BlobViolation.render() (was crashing on absolute paths outside PROJECT_ROOT, caught by the new TestMain fixtures using tmp_path), (iii) docstring claimed "218 instances" which was raw grep count not real audit — corrected to 93 with the AST-filter delta noted. False-positive audit: zero Class B (.communicate() heuristic) violations in production code, confirming the "rare outside subprocess.Popen" assumption held. PR #164's _batch_cat_blobs fix (proc.communicate(input=request, timeout=60)) is the canonical pattern this lint enforces.

    • C-2 PR-2c — useVirtualGrid grid virtualization（v2.8.0, feature, dogfoods PR #160 scaffold for third time） — closes out the C-2 軌道 by virtualizing the tenant-card grid for large sets, completing the path that PR #150 (server-side fetch / page_size cap of 500) and PR #163 (server-side q filter so we don't even hold 500 in memory unless the user wants to) opened. Even at 500 cards the DOM was heavy enough on slower devices to cause noticeable scroll jank — virtualization keeps only ~20-25 cards mounted at any time regardless of filtered.length. Self-written minimal hook (no CDN dependency on react-window — would have required updating the jsx-loader vendor list, larger blast radius than the feature warranted). useVirtualGrid({ items, rowHeight, columnCount, containerRef, overscan }) (135 lines) returns { visibleItems, totalHeight, startRow, endRow }: tracks scrollTop via a passive scroll listener on the passed container ref + containerHeight via ResizeObserver (with a clientHeight fallback for environments without it), computes the visible row range with overscan padding, and lays cards out absolute-positioned at row.top inside a full-height spacer so the scrollbar represents the entire grid. Threshold: only virtualizes when filtered.length > 50 — below threshold the orchestrator falls back to the existing CSS-grid auto-fill path, which is fast enough at small N and gives nicer responsive column counts than a fixed 3-column virtualized grid. Honest scope (PR-2c v1): fixed rowHeight: 380px (matches the tallest realistic TenantCard; shorter cards just have whitespace below, nothing clips because each card sits at its row's top with its own natural height), fixed columnCount: 3 (matches auto-fill, minmax(300px, 1fr) at typical desktop widths). Variable row heights, responsive column count from container width, and windowed key reuse are deferred to a v2 if/when needed. Module-const tuning constants (VIRTUAL_GRID_THRESHOLD / VIRTUAL_GRID_ROW_HEIGHT / VIRTUAL_GRID_COLUMN_COUNT) avoid invalidating the hook's internal useMemo per render — same stable-identity discipline as TENANT_MANAGER_URL_KEYS from PR-2b. Rules-of-Hooks discipline preserved: useVirtualGrid invoked unconditionally above the loading / error early returns (alongside modalRef = useModalFocusTrap(...) from PR-2d Phase 2), result used conditionally via enableVirtualization ternary in the render branch — same pattern as the Rules-of-Hooks fix from PR #150 commit 2caddc2. Two new e2e tests: (1) 200 synthetic tenants → asserts [data-testid="tenant-grid-virtual"] container present AND DOM card count between 1 and 60 (much less than 200 — proves virtualization engaged), (2) 10 tenants → asserts the virtualized container is absent and all 10 cards render via the plain grid path (proves the threshold gate works in both directions). Third dogfooding of PR #160 scaffold tool — make jsx-extract KIND=hook NAME=useVirtualGrid PARENT=tenant-manager auto-created the file + auto-wired dependencies: [...] + import block. Three real-world dogfoodings confirm the scaffold's design (after PR #161 TenantCard + PR #163 useDebouncedValue/useURLState). Orchestrator: 772 → 881 lines (+109 from virtualized render branch + module-const block + ref/hook wiring); still well under 1500 soft cap from PR #154 (no --strict-linecount warning from PR #162). Closes the C-2 軌道: server-side fetch (#150) + server-side q filter (#163) + DOM virtualization (this PR) — the original "500+ tenants freeze the page" problem from planning §C-2 is now addressed at all three layers.

    • C-2 PR-2b — server-side q filter + URL state（v2.8.0, feature, dogfoods PR #160 scaffold for second time） — frees tenant-manager from client-side substring-search-over-page-of-500 by delegating free-text matching to the C-1 backend's q= query param. Behavior identical — same ARIA semantics (tabIndex={0} + aria-label on article + checkbox aria-label preserved), same hover state logic (orchestrator still owns hoveredCard; TenantCard receives isHovered boolean + onHoverEnter/onHoverLeave callbacks), same Pending-PR badge (prByTenant[name] → pendingPR prop). 9-file subdirectory layout: 5 components + 2 hooks + 1 utility + 1 fixture. The orchestrator at 736 lines is now under 800; if PR-2b adds q-filter state machine and pushes back over 1500, remaining inline render blocks (ActiveFiltersBar / Modal) become next extraction candidates. The scaffold tool eliminated the 5-step boilerplate footgun perfectly — no S#67-style latent bug surface this time because the wiring was generated mechanically.

    • scaffold_jsx_dep.py + make jsx-extract — JSX multi-file scaffolder（v2.8.0, dx） — codifies the indirect-eval / window.__X self-registration pattern from PR-2d (#153 Phase 1+2 / S#69+S#70) into a code-driven scaffolding tool. The pattern was previously knowledge-in-comments; now it's a one-line command that mechanically does the five touch-points that are easy to miss when extracting a JSX module: (1) front-matter scaffold (title + purpose + register-on-window comment), (2) the actual symbol declaration (function / const / multi-symbol fixture), (3) the window.__<Name> = <Name>; self-registration at file tail, (4) appending the new path to the orchestrator's front-matter dependencies: [...] array (multi-line YAML — easy to mis-format), (5) appending const <Name> = window.__<Name>; to the orchestrator's import block. scripts/tools/dx/scaffold_jsx_dep.py supports five kinds (fixture / util / hook / component / view) mapping to <parent>/{fixtures,utils,hooks,components,views}/<name>.{js,jsx}. Validates naming convention per kind (hooks must start with use; components/views PascalCase; fixtures/utils accept kebab-case). Idempotent on re-run. --dry-run previews; --force overwrites; multi-symbol fixtures via --symbols A,B. 60 new unit tests in tests/dx/test_scaffold_jsx_dep.py cover naming validation (7) + path layout (5) + template content (12 incl. kebab auto-conversion) + symbol-derivation helpers / _is_valid_js_identifier parameterized (12) + orchestrator deps insert (6) + orchestrator imports insert (4) + end-to-end (5) + invalid---symbols rejection (1). All pass locally in ~0.45s. Pre-merge self-review on PR #160 caught and fixed a critical bug where kebab-case fixture/util names without --symbols silently generated INVALID JavaScript (const demo-foo = ... is parsed as demo minus foo and fails) — fixed by auto-converting fixture kebab → SCREAMING_SNAKE (matches the demo-tenants.js → DEMO_TENANTS convention from PR #156) and erroring out for util kebab without --symbols (util filenames like yaml-generators.js rarely map 1:1 to a single symbol). Makefile target jsx-extract wraps the script with arg-validation + a usage block printed when args missing — sits next to make platform-data / make verify-release. docs/internal/jsx-multi-file-pattern.md playbook codifies the pattern in long-form: TL;DR template, the indirect-eval const-leak rationale (S#69), the S#69 → S#70 archaeology timeline, loading-order rules, lint coverage, three common gotchas (Rules-of-Hooks ordering inside extracted hooks, multi-symbol fixtures, the 400-aspiration vs 1500-lint-cap distinction). Generated code in templates references this doc + S#69/S#70 by SHA so future readers can trace the rationale. Why this exists: PR-2d Phase 1 + 2 created 8 hand-rolled scaffolds across two PRs with the same 5-step boilerplate; S#70 self-review caught a defensive-import gap in Phase 1's GroupSidebar.jsx that would have been impossible if a tool generated the boilerplate. Scaffold-before-third-instance rule: when you've done a pattern by hand twice, the third time deserves a tool.

    • 詳見 docs/interactive/tools/tenant-manager/ directory + commit message + planning S#69

    • lint_jsx_babel.py line-count guard（v2.8.0, lint, issue #152） — codifies the lesson from PR #150 / S#67: tenant-manager.jsx accumulated 3 latent bugs over months because the 1691-line single file was too large for cross-checking useState declarations against set* references, hook ordering against early returns, and lifecycle paths in async branches. The guard adds a third validation pass to the existing JSX lint pipeline (alongside static patterns + Babel parse) — soft cap warns at 1500 lines, hard cap fails at 2500 lines under --ci. Soft-cap warnings stay non-fatal under default --ci (so commits aren't blocked during the v2.8.0 transition) and become fatal under --ci --strict. Hard-cap violations are always fatal under --ci regardless of --strict, mirroring how Babel parse errors are handled (severity-tier match: "file this big virtually guarantees latent bugs" = same blast radius as "file fails to parse"). Thresholds carry a # TODO(v2.9.0): revisit comment — they're conservative starting points (1500 picks today's single outlier tenant-manager.jsx at 1691 lines without flagging anyone else: next-largest is operator-setup-wizard.jsx at 1252; 2500 gives ~50% headroom over today's worst offender so it doesn't insta-fail current reality but blocks the next such offender). 32 new unit tests in tests/lint/test_lint_jsx_babel_linecount.py — 15 pin _run_line_count_check constants + boundary semantics (> vs >= at both caps + trailing-newline counting matches wc -l) + 17 cover the _compute_exit_code severity matrix (8-state truth table over --ci × --strict × 4 failure categories), proving the contract. Includes verbatim acceptance criteria from issue #152 (2499 warns-but-passes; 2501 fails). The guard's actionable error message points to issue #153 (PR-2d file decomposition) so future hits know the pattern to apply. Pre-commit wiring: existing jsx-babel-check hook already runs --ci, so soft-cap warns + hard-cap blocks immediately on local commit; a manual-stage --strict hook can be added in a follow-up to also surface soft-cap on CI. Refactored main() to delegate severity computation to the pure _compute_exit_code() helper so the matrix is unit-testable without disk / Node.js.

    • Phase .c — C-2 PR-2: tenant-manager.jsx API-first data source（v2.8.0） — wires the C-1 server-side search endpoint (PR #148) into the Tenant Manager UI. The JSX now tries GET /api/v1/tenants/search?page_size=500 first and falls back to platform-data.json (then DEMO_TENANTS) on any error. Addresses the planning §C-2 root cause for the 500+ tenant DOM-freeze problem: when the live API is reachable, the client never holds more than the page_size cap of summary records. UX preserves the existing client-side filter / search controls — they continue to operate over the visible set.

    • fetchTenantsFromAPI() — primary data path. Returns null on 4xx / 5xx / network error so the caller's try/catch doesn't surface confusing errors on the docs-site demo path (where there's no tenant-api in front). On 200, converts the SearchResponse {items: [TenantSummary]} shape into the existing tenants{} map keyed by id. Maps summary.maintenance → 'maintenance' first (stronger override), then summary.silent_mode → 'silent', else 'normal'.
    • fetchWithRateLimitRetry() — handles 429 once. Parses Retry-After (integer-seconds form per RFC 7231; HTTP-date form intentionally not implemented in v1 — rare for rate limits). Caps wait at 30s so a hostile server can't hang the page. Surfaces a warning-tier apiNotification toast so the user knows a retry is happening rather than thinking the page hung. Single retry — second 429 falls through to the caller, which returns null → static fallback path.
    • apiNotification extended with warning tier — was error / success only. New variant uses var(--da-color-warning-soft) background + ⏱️ icon. Used by the 429 retry toast.
    • Search-overflow banner — when API responds with total_matched > items.length (i.e. customer has > 500 tenants and we hit the page_size cap), a non-blocking banner tells the operator to refine search / filter controls until the matched set fits. Bilingual zh + en. Style consts extracted to satisfy lint_jsx_babel.py (no style={{ ... }} literals).
    • loadGroupsBestEffort() — in API mode, groups still come from platform-data.json (the tenant-api doesn't yet expose group definitions; they live in _groups.yaml adjacent to the tenants). Falls back to DEMO_GROUPS when neither is reachable. Documented as a known gap; full group-API exposure is a future PR.
    • dataSource state — exposes 'api' | 'static' | 'demo' for diagnostics + tests.
    • 3 new Playwright e2e tests (tests/e2e/tenant-manager.spec.ts) — happy-path API mode (page.route() mocked 200 with 2 tenants → both render); overflow banner (mock total_matched: 2000 / items: 500 → banner contains both numbers + "refine"/"narrow" hint); 429 retry (mock 429 with Retry-After: 1 → retry → 200 → callCount ≥ 2 + post-retry tenant in DOM).
    • Honest scope (explicit non-goals, deferred to future PRs)：server-side filter (debounced text → query param q) — current PR keeps client-side useMemo filter intact running over the ≤500-item visible set; URL state mgmt (URLSearchParams sync) for bookmark sharing; per-row prefetch on scroll for paginated browsing > 500 tenants; virtualization (react-window or inline) for the multi-column variable-height card grid — substantial separate design work; live groups API surface (currently still platform-data.json fallback).
    • Why "PR-2 v1" not "PR-2 final"：planning §C-2 calls out "server-side search + virtualized list + URL state + bookmark sharing" as the full scope. This PR ships the data-source layer (the highest-impact piece — addresses the root cause of 500+ tenant DOM freeze by capping payload size at server). UI/UX evolution layered on top can ship incrementally without breaking this contract.

    • Phase .c — C-1 Server-side tenant search API (PR-1 of C-1+C-2+C-2a UI bundle)（v2.8.0） — new endpoint GET /api/v1/tenants/search for the v2.8.0 Tenant Manager UI overhaul (C-2 / C-2a deferred to follow-up PRs). Replaces the all-or-nothing client-side filter that freezes the React DOM at 500+ tenant scale; supports pagination, exact-match metadata filters, free-text substring search, and deterministic sort. Reuses the existing rate-limit (PR #135 / Track C) + RBAC + RequestID middleware so the surface is bounded by the same 100 req/min per-caller budget the rest of tenant-api enforces.

    • SearchTenants handler (components/tenant-api/internal/handler/tenant_search.go)：query params q (free-text substring, case-insensitive — matches id / owner / domain / db_type / tags[]), environment / tier / domain / db_type (exact-match filters, AND-ed), tag (single exact-match in _metadata.tags), page_size (default 50, hard cap 500), offset (≥ 0), sort (id default / environment / tier / domain — id is ALWAYS the secondary tiebreaker so pagination is deterministic). Response: {items, total_matched, page_size, next_offset} (next_offset null on last page).
    • tenantSnapshotCache in-memory cache w/ 30s TTL — first request after expiry rebuilds from disk (loadAllTenants), subsequent requests serve from memory + filter / sort. At 1000-tenant scale the post-cache filter+sort is sub-ms; cache miss is a one-time disk scan amortized across the next 30s window. p99 latency budget ≤ 200ms (planning §C-1) comfortably met. Watch-based invalidation deferred (file watcher coupling is a separate concern; 30s staleness acceptable for UI search).
    • Built-in defenses (planning §C-1)：(i) hard page_size ≤ 500 cap (excess returns structured 400 + page_size exceeds max 500 message)；(ii) free-text search restricted to a closed list of indexed fields — full-tree YAML scan is rejected as DoS vector + would surface internal metadata；(iii) RBAC filter applied BEFORE pagination so total_matched reflects what the caller could ever reach by paging (not a global count that leaks tenant existence)；(iv) inherits the 100 req/min rate-limit + RequestID echo from PR #135.
    • cmd/server/main.go wires the new route under /api/v1/tenants/search with the same rbacMgr.Middleware(rbac.PermRead, nil) chain as /api/v1/tenants — RBAC PermRead required, no per-tenant ID match needed (list endpoint).
    • Honest scope (PR-1 of C-1+C-2+C-2a)：純後端 + tests，不動 frontend。Deferred to PR-2 (C-2)：Tenant Manager JSX react-window virtualization + URL state + 429 retry-with-backoff toast wiring this endpoint。Deferred to PR-3 (C-2a)：API contract testing — record real /effective schema → tenant_effective.schema.json + replace tests/e2e/fixtures/mock-data.ts mock shape. Also deferred: cursor-style opaque pagination tokens (numeric offset suffices for v1), watch-based cache invalidation (30s TTL acceptable), inverted index for fuzzy free-text (closed-field substring suffices).
    • 19 new tests tests/handler/tenant_search_test.go (-race -count=2 穩定)：default page (3) + sort-by-id-asc-default + 3-page pagination determinism (no gaps / no dups across page boundaries) + offset-past-end empty + 5 error paths (page_size > 500 / negative page_size / negative offset / unknown sort key / non-numeric page_size) + environment exact-match filter + AND-ed multi-filter + tag exact-match (kept distinct from free-text) + free-text matches id/owner/domain + free-text case-insensitive (3 cases) + free-text matches tags + RBAC filter applied before pagination (production-realistic — wraps handler in real rbac.Middleware to populate identity context, not just header) + snapshot cache reuse-during-TTL + rebuilds-after-TTL + invalidate-forces-rebuild
    • C-1+C-2+C-2a UI 軌道：PR-1 完成（this PR）→ PR-2 JSX virtualization + state mgmt (~1.5 週) → PR-3 contract testing (~0.5 週)。下一步 follow-up：PR-2 開新 branch 接這個 endpoint

    • Phase .c — C-11 PR-3 Layer 1: cosign keyless signing + SBOM (supply-chain Layer 1)（v2.8.0） — every tools/v* Release artefact (binaries / Docker image / air-gapped tar / SBOM / SHA256SUMS) now ships with cosign keyless signatures (sigstore ecosystem) and an SBOM in both SPDX and CycloneDX formats. Customers can cryptographically verify that an artefact came from THIS repo's release.yaml workflow at the requested tag — not just "unmodified in transit" (sha256 already proved that), but "signed by the release pipeline".

    • Layered design rationale：not all customers need the same scheme; pre-doing 4 signing paths (cosign / GPG / Authenticode / FIPS-HSM) creates compound maintenance cost + permanent contracts that can't be cleanly unwound. Solution: ship Layer 1 (cosign keyless + SBOM, the cloud-native baseline ~70-80% customers accept) by default, Layer 2 (GPG / Authenticode) deferred behind customer-driven activation, Layer 3 (HSM / SLSA Level 2-3 / FIPS) gated on actual RFP. Full design + activation paths in docs/internal/release-signing-runbook.md.
    • release.yaml additions：(a) id-token: write permission (OIDC keyless prerequisite); (b) cosign installer (sigstore/cosign-installer@v3.7.0 pinning cosign v2.4.1) + syft installer (anchore/sbom-action/download-syft@v0.17.7 pinning syft v1.18.1); (c) sign Docker image by digest (immutable, not by tag); (d) generate SBOM SPDX + CycloneDX for the Docker image; (e) sign SBOM files (tampered SBOM defeats supply chain); (f) sign every binary archive + zip + SHA256SUMS index + air-gapped image tar with cosign sign-blob; (g) Release upload step extended to include all .sig / .cert / SBOM files.
    • scripts/tools/dx/verify_release.sh — friendly customer-facing helper that runs the full sha256 + cosign chain end-to-end. Auto-downloads artefact + sig + cert + SHA256SUMS if not local; verifies sha256 against index; verifies cosign signature with certificate-identity pinned to our release.yaml workflow path at the requested tag. Exit codes: 0 verified / 1 verification failed / 2 caller error. Falls back gracefully when sha256sum / shasum-a-256 differ between Linux + macOS. 14 tests (tests/dx/test_verify_release.py) covering arg parsing, missing tools, mock-cosign happy + failure paths, sha256 mismatch + match flows, quiet mode.
    • make verify-release — Makefile target wrapping the helper for one-line interactive verification. Usage: make verify-release TAG=tools/v2.8.0 ARTEFACT=da-parser-linux-amd64.tar.gz.
    • Customer-facing docs (docs/migration-toolkit-installation.{md,en.md})：new ## Signature Verification section with three flows — (a) quick verification via our helper script; (b) manual cosign verify-blob command for customer CI to pin (don't depend on our script); (c) Docker image cosign verify; (d) SBOM format mapping (SPDX for FedRAMP / NIST workflows, CycloneDX for OWASP-stack tools); (e) air-gapped verification path (TUF mirror pre-sync OR --insecure-ignore-tlog degraded mode). Bilingual zh + en.
    • Internal runbook docs/internal/release-signing-runbook.md — maintainer-facing layered design doc：Layer 1 active state + failure modes + recovery; Layer 2 customer-driven activation paths (GPG / Authenticode / dual-signing) with concrete release.yaml stubs ready to enable; Layer 3 explicit non-goal list (HSM / FIPS / SLSA Level 2-3 / reproducible builds / in-toto / 21 CFR Part 11 / region-specific CAs); maintainer onboarding checklist.
    • Customer activation issue template .github/ISSUE_TEMPLATE/signing-request.md — structured template for customer security teams to request Layer 2 / 3 schemes. Forces the asker to identify their actual compliance driver (FedRAMP / NIST / DORA / etc.) and use case before maintainer commits effort.
    • Honest scope (explicit non-goals)：no GPG signing / no Windows Authenticode / no HSM-backed keys / no SLSA Level 2-3 / no reproducible builds / no in-toto attestation chain / no FIPS 140-2 / no region-specific CA chains. Each is a separately-scoped Layer 2 / Layer 3 activation gated on real customer demand. The runbook documents how to wire each one in WHEN that demand appears.
    • Why this is "Layer 1" not "everything"：cosign keyless (sigstore + Rekor transparency log) is the current cloud-native industry default. It works without long-term private key management, requires no annual cert payment, no key rotation procedures, no maintainer-handover key transfer choreography. It covers the most commonly asked compliance frameworks (NIST SSDF) for cloud-native customers. Layer 2 schemes have specific niches (GPG for air-gapped + customers refusing sigstore transparency model; Authenticode for native Windows binaries with Smart Screen blocking) and bring permanent operational cost (key custody, cert renewals, dual-document maintenance) — done only when a real customer asks.

    • 詳見 docs/internal/release-signing-runbook.md / planning §12.2 Phase .c row C-11

    • Phase .c — C-9 Profile Builder PR-5 — fuzzy matching (duration-equivalence ConfidenceMedium proposals)（v2.8.0） — closes the C-9 軌道 by adding the long-deferred "fuzzier matching pass" that planning §C-9 PR-1 opening comments and S#56 PR-4 lessons flagged. Strict (PR-1) clustering only merges rules with EXACT signature match; fuzzy adds a second pass that collapses duration-equivalent expressions (rate(foo[5m]) ≡ rate(foo[300s]) ≡ rate(foo[300000ms])) into ConfidenceMedium proposals.

    • canonicaliseDurations() (internal/profile/normalize.go) — rewrites every [<duration>] literal to a digit-free placeholder [<DUR_<base26-encoded-millis>>]. Two raw expressions whose only difference is duration syntax produce byte-identical normalised output. Multi-unit forms (1h30m, 2h45m30s) and the standard PromQL unit set {y, w, d, h, m, s, ms} all canonicalise correctly. Unparseable forms left verbatim (better to under-merge than silently collapse a token we can't fully parse). Letters-only encoding survives the existing numericLiteral / quotedString passes
    • normaliseExpr variadic options — WithCanonicalDurations() toggles the duration pass without breaking PR-1 callers (no args = strict). Future fuzzy axes extend the option pattern without API breakage
    • Two-pass BuildProposals() (internal/profile/cluster.go) — Pass 1 strict (today's behaviour, ConfidenceHigh); Pass 2 fuzzy on the strict-residue using duration-canonicalised signatures (ConfidenceMedium). Strict pass always wins: rules in strict clusters never feed fuzzy, protecting high-confidence proposals from contamination
    • ClusterOptions.EnableFuzzy bool — opt-in (default false), preserves PR-1 backward compat for existing callers (da-tools profile, simulate-time builders). Migration-time customer corpus processing should set true to capture the duration-equivalent collapses that strict mode misses
    • Hard guarantees：fuzzy NEVER crosses dialects (vendor-lock-in risk; prom ≠ metricsql), fuzzy NEVER merges across for: variance (usually intentional alert-tier separation), fuzzy NEVER alters proposal SharedExprTemplate shape (still a real-rule render, not the synthetic placeholder)
    • Honest scope (explicit non-goals)：no for:-variance pass (different for: = different alert intent), no Levenshtein label fuzzy matching, no AST-level structural matching, no comment stripping, no offset-duration canonicalisation (rare in customer corpora). Each future axis deserves its own design + test pass
    • 21 new tests -race -count=2 穩定 — duration parsing (8 cases incl. 100ms / 1h30m / 2h45m30s) + base26 encoding (round-trip + uniqueness for n=0..999 + negative defensive) + canonicalisation equivalence (5m=300s=300000ms, 1h=60m, 1h30m=90m, different durations stay different, identifier preservation) + variadic option backward compat (no args = strict) + 12 cluster behaviour tests (off-preserves-PR-1 / on-collapses / strict-wins / no-cross-dialect / no-cross-for / deterministic JSON / mixed high+medium output sort by member-id not tier / singleton residue / signature contract / fuzzy reason text)
    • emit.go unchanged — already plumbs prop.Confidence through to PROPOSAL.md headers + JSON; medium-confidence proposals render naturally with the new tier label
    • C-9 軌道完結（PR-1 cluster engine + extraction proposals → PR-2 emission → PR-3 translator + ADR-019 → PR-4 accept/reject decisions → PR-5 fuzzy matching）

    • 詳見 cluster.go 包頭 / normalize.go PR-5 design notes / planning §12.2 Phase .c row C-9

    • Phase .c — C-8 PromRule parser PR-2 + customer CLI surface bundle（v2.8.0） — completes the C-8 軌道 by turning the PR-1 parser library into a customer-runnable binary with the anti-vendor-lock-in promise wired through. Bundled with the parser CLI integration (build.sh / Dockerfile / release matrix / Python dispatcher / docs) so reviewers see one coherent customer flow rather than 5 fragmented "wire da-parser into surface X" PRs:

    • vm_only_functions.yaml externalised (components/threshold-exporter/app/internal/parser/) — the VM-only function allowlist moves from a hardcoded Go map to a YAML file embedded via go:embed. Single source of truth for "what makes a rule MetricsQL-only"; updates no longer require Go source edits, and the new metricsql_version: pin lets a freshness gate detect drift
    • Freshness CI gate (vm_only_functions_freshness_test.go) — fails when metricsql_version: in the YAML doesn't match the metricsql require line in go.mod. Coverage-floor + core-entries-present sub-tests catch corrupt/regressed allowlist edits. When the metricsql dep is bumped, this test forces a re-audit of the upstream changelog before merge
    • StrictPromQLValidator (strict_prom.go) — runs prometheus/promql/parser.NewParser(Options{}).ParseExpr per rule. New ParseOptions{StrictPromQL: bool} toggles it; ParsePromRules (PR-1 contract) preserves zero-value behaviour for backward compat. Singleton parser instance (sync.Once) — process-wide reuse for tight CLI loops
    • ParsedRule.PromCompatible: bool + StrictPromError: string new schema fields — finer signal than prom_portable (which only checks "no VM-only function names"). A rule can be dialect=prom but prom_compatible=false if metricsql happens to accept a shape Prometheus rejects; customers running --fail-on-non-portable rely on this to gate migrations
    • cmd/da-parser/ — new Go binary mirroring da-guard / da-batchpr patterns. Subcommands: import (parse YAML → JSON ParseResult, with --validate-strict-prom default-on, --fail-on-non-portable, --fail-on-ambiguous portability gates) + allowlist (introspect the embedded VM-only allowlist as text or JSON). Stable exit codes 0/1/2. cmdX → runX testable split same as da-batchpr
    • scripts/tools/ops/parser_dispatch.py — Python wrapper mirroring batchpr_dispatch.py. Subcommand IS preserved in forward_args (vs guard_dispatch which strips it). Binary resolution: --da-parser-binary <path> → $DA_PARSER_BINARY → da-parser on $PATH → friendly install hint
    • components/da-tools/app/entrypoint.py — COMMAND_MAP entries "parser": "parser_dispatch.py" AND "batch-pr": "batchpr_dispatch.py" (the latter was advertised by PR #133 but never actually wired to entrypoint; this bundle fixes that drift) + bilingual help text sections for both
    • build.sh + Dockerfile — da-parser bundled into the da-tools Docker image at /usr/local/bin/da-parser alongside da-guard + da-batchpr. build.sh's TOOL_FILES gains both parser_dispatch.py and the previously-missing batchpr_dispatch.py (test_command_map_scripts_in_build_sh would have caught the latter on next test run)
    • release.yaml cross-compile matrix — extended from 12 binaries (6 da-guard + 6 da-batchpr) to 18 (adds 6 da-parser). SHA256SUMS includes all 18; for BIN in da-guard da-batchpr da-parser outer loop keeps the matrix DRY

    • cmd/da-batchpr/ (new Go binary, 4 source files + 4 test files) — subcommand dispatcher + 3 verbs:
      • da-batchpr apply --plan plan.json --emit-dir ./emit/ --repo owner/name --workdir ./repo — opens or updates tenant chunk PRs from a Plan + C-9 emit output. CLI walks --emit-dir recursively and calls batchpr.AllocateFiles(plan, files) to bucket per-PlanItem before invoking batchpr.Apply()

    • Stable exit codes：0 clean / 1 per-target failures (or refresh conflicts) / 2 caller error (bad flags, missing/invalid path, IO failure, JSON parse error). Mirrors the da-guard contract for CI script consistency
    • JSON-input-first contract：each subcommand's primary input is a JSON file (or stdin via --input -); reports + machine-readable results write to file (--report / --result-json) or stdout. The smart parts (parse + cluster + emit + cross-ref) live above batchpr in C-8 / C-9 and the Python da-tools wrapper; convenience flags (e.g. --base-merged-sha for refresh) deferred to a future CLI-polish PR
    • Testable architecture (cmdX → runX split)：each subcommand has a production dispatcher (cmdApply/cmdRefresh/cmdRefreshSource) that parses flags + constructs production clients (ShellGitClient + GHPRClient), and a testable core (runApply etc.) that takes injected batchpr.GitClient+batchpr.PRClient.     • Phase .c — C-10 Batch PR Pipeline PR-4 — refresh --source-rule-ids mode (data-layer hot-fix path)（v2.8.0） — closes the orthogonal half of the C-10 refresh story PR-3 opened. PR-3 handles "Base PR merged → tenant branches need rebase"; PR-4 handles "Parser bug fix changes how N source rules translate → only those N rules' derived files need re-emitting". Canonical scenario from planning §C-10:

      parser tools/v2.8.0 → tools/v2.8.1 fixes a histogram bucket off-by-one bug. The fix changes how 200 source rules out of the customer's 10 000-rule corpus translate to threshold-exporter conf.d shape. Without PR-4 the fix means re-running the FULL apply pipeline; PR-4 ships the surgical "patch only what changed" path.

    • RefreshSource() orchestration (internal/batchpr/refresh_source.go) — same per-target failure-isolation + context-cancellation + inter-call-delay shape as PR-3's Refresh(). Per-target pipeline: GetPR (state check) → empty-files-check → checkout → write → commit → push → comment. Distinct from Refresh(): PR-4 adds a NEW commit on top of the existing tenant branch (regular Push, not force-push) — preserving history so ongoing reviewer conversations don't break
    • State-aware skip + no-change skip — closed/merged PRs (PatchSkippedClosed) and tenants whose Files map is empty (PatchSkippedNoChange, the caller's diff produced nothing for this tenant) are recorded distinctly so the report shows what was considered vs what was abandoned. Optional PostCommentOnSkipped flag for audit-trail customers
    • GitClient interface extended — CheckoutBranch(ctx, branch) switches to an EXISTING tenant branch (NOT reset, distinct from CreateBranch which git checkout -B resets to a base). Production impl runs git fetch origin → git checkout <branch>; surfaces missing-branch as a hard error since PR-4 callers always reference a real, open tenant PR
    • patch-plan.md markdown generator — header (repo / mode / target count / unique source rule count) + summary counts + per-PR outcomes table (PR / branch / state / status / files / notes) + Source-rules → tenant PRs cross-reference (one row per unique source rule ID showing all PRs it touches; helpful when one hot-fix affects many tenants and the reviewer wants the inverse mapping). Stable across runs given the same input
    • Caller-driven file content (honest layering) — caller (CLI / UI in PR-5) does the heavy lifting: re-parse with new parser → re-cluster → cross-reference source_rule_id ↔ tenant PR ↔ proposal → re-emit affected files → hand batchpr typed RefreshSourceTarget per tenant with the new content. Putting the cross-ref + emit inside batchpr would pull C-8 parser + C-9 profile/emit as deps, violating the layering. Same pattern as PR-3 — caller passes typed targets; batchpr orchestrates the I/O dance
    • Source rule IDs flow into commit message + comment — <source-rule-ids> placeholder in CommitMessageOverride / CommentBody substituted with comma-joined IDs. Default messages: commit "Data-layer hot-fix: re-emitted source rules X, Y, Z." + comment "Data-layer hot-fix applied for source rules X, Y, Z — please re-review the latest commit." Long ID lists truncate to "first, second, ... + N more" cap at ~120 chars to keep commit subjects + comment bodies readable
    • 28 new tests / -race -count=2 穩定 — 5 input validation paths / empty-targets-no-op / happy all-updated (with file-count assertion + commit/push/comment counts) / file-content-reaches-git-client invariant (pins caller's bytes flow verbatim into GitClient.WriteFiles, no transform) / empty-files marks no-change while batch continues / closed PR skip / merged PR skip / PostCommentOnSkipped flag / DryRun (no remote work, FilesUpdated still populated for "would patch N files" report) / 6 step failures (get_pr / checkout / write / commit / push / comment with "commit + push DID succeed" hint + FilesUpdated populated on comment-only failure) / one-failure-doesnt-sink-batch / custom commit-msg + comment-body with <source-rule-ids> substitution / empty SourceRuleIDs handled gracefully (no dangling "for source rules" prefix) / context cancellation / report includes Per-PR + Source-rules cross-ref / shared-rule-across-targets correctly merges in cross-ref / joinSourceRuleIDs truncate + single-very-long-ID passthrough

PR-4 doesn't auto-discover affected PRs from source rule IDs (caller passes the typed list), doesn't implement the parser+emit re-run (caller does it), doesn't auto-resolve conflicts (the patch is a regular commit, no rebase here)

    • 詳見 internal/batchpr/refresh_source.go package header / planning §12.2 Phase .c row C-10

    • Phase .c — C-10 Batch PR Pipeline PR-3 — refresh --base-merged mode (Rebase Hell solver)（v2.8.0） — closes the auto-rebase loop after a Base Infrastructure PR merges. Without PR-3, the M tenant chunk PRs C-10 PR-2 opened against pre-merge main now show their diff as if it includes the Base PR's _defaults.yaml content (already in main!) — reviewers can't distinguish what's new from what's already-merged. PR-3 walks the tenant PR list in batch, rebases each branch onto the merged main HEAD, force-pushes-with-lease, and posts a "rebased onto merged Base PR" comment so reviewers see the refresh happened.

    • Refresh() orchestration (internal/batchpr/refresh.go) — same architectural pattern as Apply(): per-target pipeline (GetPR → state check → RebaseOnto → ForcePushWithLease → CommentPR), per-target failure isolation (one bad PR doesn't sink the batch), context-cancellation aware, optional inter-call delay for GitHub secondary rate-limit softening
    • State-aware skip logic — closed/merged tenant PRs surface as RebaseSkippedClosed (no rebase attempted; reviewer's intent already executed). PostCommentOnSkipped flag lets callers post a courtesy "skipped (PR closed)" comment if their workflow needs the audit trail
    • Conflict handling — RebaseOnto on conflict: git status --porcelain parsed for conflicted-file list, git rebase --abort runs to leave working tree clean, RebaseOutcome.Conflicted=true returned. Orchestration records RebaseConflicts status with ConflictedFiles populated; tenant PR is left untouched (no force-push, no comment) so the reviewer can do the manual rebase. Generated refresh-report.md includes a Conflicts section listing files per PR + suggested manual git rebase --onto command
    • GitClient interface extended — RebaseOnto(ctx, branch, oldBase, newBase) (*RebaseOutcome, error) + ForcePushWithLease(ctx, branch) error. Conflicts are an outcome, not an interface error — the orchestration distinguishes "rebase couldn't even start" (network / repo missing) from "started but conflicts emerged"
    • PRClient interface extended — GetPR(ctx, num) (*PRDetails, error) returning {Number, State, HeadBranch, URL} with normalised PRState (open/closed/merged/unknown — merged distinct from closed so Refresh can tell success from abandonment) + CommentPR(ctx, num, body) for the success / skip notes
    • Production shell-out impls：ShellGitClient.RebaseOnto runs git fetch origin → git checkout <branch> → git rebase --onto <newBase> <oldBase> <branch>, parses conflicts via git status --porcelain, aborts cleanly. ShellGitClient.ForcePushWithLease uses --force-with-lease (refuses to overwrite remote work landed since fetch — safer than plain --force). GHPRClient.GetPR shells gh pr view <num> --json number,state,headRefName,url with state upper-case→lower-case normalisation. GHPRClient.CommentPR shells gh pr comment <num> --body <body>
    • refresh-report.md markdown generator — header (repo / Base PR / merge SHA / mode) + summary counts + per-PR table (PR number, branch, state, status, notes) + Conflicts section with suggested manual commands + Warnings section. Always populated, even for empty Targets (logs "no PRs needed refresh; refresh is a no-op" so a scheduled cron job's output is audibly meaningful)
    • 24 new tests / -race -count=2 穩定 — 7 input validation paths / empty-targets-no-op / happy all-clean / conflicts (recorded + report has files + suggested manual commands) / closed PR skip / merged PR skip / PostCommentOnSkipped flag / DryRun (no remote work, no comments) / 4 step-failures (get_pr / rebase / push / comment with "rebase succeeded" hint) / one-failure-doesnt-sink-batch / custom CommentBody with <base-sha> substitution / context cancellation marks all unprocessed as failed / report includes Base PR number + short SHA / report fall-back to short SHA when no PR number / shortSHA helper truncate + passthrough
    • Honest scope discipline — PR-3 DOES execute the rebase + push (full Rebase Hell automation, not just diagnosis). Out of scope: refresh --source-rule-ids for data-layer hot-fixes (PR-4 territory; depends on C-8 parser provenance); auto-resolve heuristics for common conflict patterns (manual rebase remains the human's job for now); discovery via PR-description scan (caller passes typed RefreshTarget list — typically constructed from PR-2's ApplyResult — so we never string-scrape "Blocked by" text)
    • Interface contract change — GitClient and PRClient (in internal/batchpr/) gain methods. Internal package, so no external consumers; downstream callers (the future da-tools batch-pr CLI in PR-5) reference the production impls anyway

    • Phase .b — Track B: B-5 Mixed-mode 驗證（v2.8.0, route C strict-plan closure plan Track B） — 在 v2.7.0 起一直支援但從未系統性測試的「flat <root>/<id>.yaml + hierarchical <root>/<dir>/<id>.yaml 並存」mixed mode 加 5 個 manager-level invariant tests + 4 個 mixed-mode benchmarks + 一份雙語客戶決策文件。零 production code 變動。

    • Phase .c — C-9 Profile Builder PR-4：accept/reject decisions filter（v2.8.0） — adds the human-in-the-loop primitive that ADR-019 §non-goals defers to a reviewer. Keeps the emission pipeline pure-Go (no UI dependency) by treating the accept/reject decision as a small YAML file the emitter can scaffold and re-consume:

    • ProposalDecision + ProposalDecisions types (internal/profile/decisions.go) — one row per cluster carrying decision: accept|reject|pending plus reviewer-cross-reference fields (member_rule_ids, summary, free-form note). File-level undecided_policy: emit|skip controls how proposals with no decision (or pending verdict) get treated
    • ExtractionProposal.Key() stable identifier — SHA-256 over SharedExprTemplate || \x00 || sorted MemberRuleIDs. Stable across runs as long as cluster identity is stable; shifts when members enter/leave or expression normalisation changes (and the emitter warns when a recorded decision references a now-stale key)
    • ScaffoldDecisions(set) → *ProposalDecisions — builds an all-pending starter file from a ProposalSet. Defensive-copies MemberRuleIDs so caller mutation can't leak into the scaffold
    • ParseDecisions / EncodeDecisions — YAML byte-level codec, deterministic output, header comment explaining edit conventions, empty input tolerated (returns empty struct rather than error)
    • EmissionInput.Decisions filter (nil = backward compat) — EmitProposals skips rejected proposals, emits accepted ones, applies the policy to undecided/pending. Pre-existing PR-2/PR-3 callers see ZERO behaviour change. Member-list drift (recorded vs live) and stale keys (decision references a cluster no longer in the set) surface as warnings without overriding the verdict
    • EmissionInput.EmitDecisionsScaffold flag — when true, drops a proposal-decisions.yaml at RootPrefix's root alongside per-proposal artifacts so reviewers see the file format up-front
    • Duplicate-key + unknown-verdict surfacing — copy-paste edits / typos warn rather than silently let the last entry win or fall through. Gives reviewers a chance to fix decisions before the next emit
    • 19 new tests / 62 total profile tests -race -count=2 穩定，含 Key stability + member-drift / scaffold round-trip + defensive copy / parse-empty + parse-malformed / accept-reject / pending+policy / missing+policy / stale-key / member-drift / unknown-verdict / duplicate-key / empty-key / EmitProposals integration (filter + scaffold + backward-compat)

    • Honest scope discipline：fuzzy clustering (medium / low confidence proposals) deferred to a future PR. PR-4 ships ONLY the accept/reject loop primitive — the smallest unit that turns the C-9 pipeline from "preview-everything" into "ship-only-what-the-reviewer-accepted". No CLI / JSX UI in this PR; future PR adds those as thin wrappers around the file-based contract
